# Investigation: DRA AllocationMode API Change Impact Analysis

**Repository:** kubernetes/kubernetes
**Task Type:** Impact Analysis (investigation only — no code changes)

## Scenario

The Dynamic Resource Allocation (DRA) scheduler plugin is being modified to allow `AllocationMode: All` from multi-node resource pools. Previously, this allocation mode was restricted to single-node pools only. Before this change ships, the team needs a comprehensive impact analysis.

## Your Task

Produce an impact analysis report at `/logs/agent/investigation.md`.

Your report MUST cover:
1. All source files that reference `AllocationMode` or the DRA allocation logic
2. Which controllers and schedulers are affected
3. What test files cover the current allocation behavior
4. What performance implications exist (scheduler hot paths affected)
5. Which downstream consumers (kubelet, device plugins) would see changed behavior
6. Risk assessment: what could break if this change has bugs

## Output Requirements

Write your investigation report to `/logs/agent/investigation.md` with these sections:

```
# Investigation Report

## Summary
<1-2 sentence finding>

## Root Cause
<Scope of the change — what components are affected and why>

## Evidence
<Code references with file paths and line numbers>

## Affected Components
<List of packages/modules impacted, categorized by risk level>

## Recommendation
<Risk mitigation strategy and testing plan>
```

## Constraints

- Do NOT write any code
- Do NOT modify any source files
- Your job is investigation and analysis only
- Focus on tracing `AllocationMode` through the DRA plugin, scheduler framework, and kubelet

143-assistanttext-
The investigation report has been written to `/logs/agent/investigation.md`. Here's a brief summary of the key findings:

**The change (commit 2e534d6) was already reverted (commit a0e500a) due to a confirmed performance regression.** However, the local working tree still has the original change applied.

Key findings:

1. **Core change:** `GatherPools()` in 3 allocator variants was modified to pre-scan **all** ResourceSlices in the cluster (not just node-matching ones) to determine global pool completeness — needed for correctness when `AllocationMode: All` spans multi-node pools.

2. **Performance impact:** `GatherPools()` runs inside `Allocate()`, which is called per-node during the scheduler's `Filter` extension point. The O(S) pre-scan over all slices multiplied by N nodes = O(S×N) total work per scheduling cycle.

3. **Affected components:** The structured allocator (stable/incubating/experimental variants), the DRA scheduler plugin's Filter path, and indirectly the quota evaluator. The kubelet DRA manager is not affected (allocation-mode agnostic).

4. **Test coverage:** One unit test was added (`"allocation-mode-all-with-multi-host-resource-pool"`); existing tests cover single-node All mode and incomplete pools.

5. **Recommendation:** Move the pre-scan into `NewAllocator()` (called once in PreFilter) rather than `Allocate()` (called per-node in Filter) to amortize the cost.

        

      

      

        Tool Calls (61)

(listed in ascending order of the number of covered test cases)\\n2: #\\n3: # - integration-test: test cases to run as the integration test, usually to spot some issues in the scheduler implementation or scheduler-perf itself.\\n4: # - performance: test cases to run in the performance test.\\n5: # - short: supplemental label for the above two labels (must not used alone), which literally means short execution time test cases.\\n6: #\\n7: # Specifically, the CIs use labels like the following:\\n8: # - `ci-kubernetes-integration-master` (`integration-test`): Test cases are chosen based on a tradeoff between code coverage and overall runtime. \\n9: # It basically covers all test cases but with their smallest workload. \\n10: # - `pull-kubernetes-integration` (`integration-test`,`short`): Test cases are chosen so that they should take less than total 5 min to complete.\\n11: # - `ci-benchmark-scheduler-perf` (`performance`): Long enough test cases are chosen (ideally, longer than 10 seconds) \\n12: # to provide meaningful samples for the pod scheduling rate.\\n13: #\\n14: # Also, `performance`+`short` isn't used in the CIs, but it's used to test the performance test locally.\\n15: # (Sometimes, the test cases with `integration-test` are too small to spot issues.)\\n16: #\\n17: # Combining `performance` and `short` selects suitable workloads for a local\\n18: # before/after comparisons with benchstat.\\n19: \\n20: # PublishResourceSlices measures how quickly the scheduler consumes ResourceSlices as they\\n21: # get created by a DRA driver. Input
{
  "content": "# Investigation Report\n\n## Summary\n\nThe change to allow `AllocationMode: All` from multi-node resource pools (commit 2e534d6) modifies the `GatherPools` function in the DRA structured allocator to pre-compute pool completeness across **all** slices (including those not targeting the current node) before filtering. This affects the scheduler's Filter extension point hot path, where `Allocate()` is called for every candidate node. The change was already reverted (commit a0e500a) due to a confirmed performance regression, indicating that the current approach of iterating all slices upfront in `GatherPools` is too expensive for the scheduler's per-node evaluation loop.\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe change modifies `GatherPools` in three allocator variants (stable, incubating, experimental) to:\n\n1. **Pre-index all slices by pool** (`slicesByPool` map) before any node filtering, adding an O(S) pass over all slices where S = total slices in the cluster.\n2. **Pre-compute incomplete pools** by checking slice counts and generations across all slices per pool, adding another O(S) pass.\n3. **Change the `IsIncomplete` check** from a local per-pool check (`len(pool.Slices) != ResourceSliceCount`) to a lookup into the pre-computed `incompletePools` set.\n\nThe core problem: previously, `GatherPools` would only process slices matching the target node. The change forces it to process **all** slices to determine global pool completeness, which is necessary for correctness (a multi-node pool with `AllocationMode: All` needs to know if the pool is complete globally, not just for one node's slices). However, this work scales with the total number of ResourceSlices in the cluster, not just those relevant to a node, and it runs on **every** `Filter` call \u2014 i.e., for every (pod, node) pair during scheduling.\n\n## Evidence\n\n### Core Change: Pool Completeness Check (3 files, identical change)\n\n**File: `staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/stable/pools_stable.go:48-95`** (local)\n- New `poolIdentifier` struct at line 48\n- `slicesByPool` pre-indexing at lines 59-65\n- `incompletePools` pre-computation at lines 71-95\n- `IsIncomplete` now uses `incompletePools.Has()` at line 143 instead of `int64(len(pool.Slices)) != pool.Slices[0].Spec.Pool.ResourceSliceCount`\n\n**Same change replicated in:**\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/incubating/pools_incubating.go`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/experimental/pools_experimental.go`\n\n### Scheduler Hot Path \u2014 Where GatherPools Is Called\n\n**File: `staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/stable/allocator_stable.go:110-134`**\n- `Allocate()` calls `GatherPools()` at line 129 for every node evaluation\n- The `Allocator` is created once in `PreFilter` (dynamicresources.go:566) but `Allocate()` is called per-node in `Filter` (dynamicresources.go:715)\n\n**File: `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/dynamicresources/dynamicresources.go:631-744`**\n- `Filter()` at line 631 is the scheduler extension point\n- Calls `state.allocator.Allocate(allocCtx, node, claimsToAllocate)` at line 715\n- This runs for **every** node in the cluster during the filter phase\n\n### AllocationMode: All Logic in Allocator\n\n**File: `staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/stable/allocator_stable.go:446-481`**\n- When `AllocationMode` is `All`, the allocator iterates `pool.DeviceSlicesTargetingNode` (line 463) to pre-collect all matching devices\n- At line 456, it checks `pool.IsIncomplete` and returns an error if true \u2014 this is where multi-node pool completeness matters\n- At lines 860-914, the actual allocation loop for \"All\" mode uses the pre-collected `allDevices` list\n\n### API Type Definitions\n\n**File: `pkg/apis/resource/types.go:1086-1092`**\n```go\ntype DeviceAllocationMode string\nconst (\n    DeviceAllocationModeExactCount = DeviceAllocationMode(\"ExactCount\")\n    DeviceAllocationModeAll        = DeviceAllocationMode(\"All\")\n)\n```\n\nIdentical definitions in:\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1/types.go:1143-1150`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1beta1/types.go:1160-1167`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1beta2/types.go:1149-1156`\n\n### Validation\n\n**File: `pkg/apis/resource/validation/validation.go:268-286`**\n- `validateDeviceAllocationMode()` validates that `AllocationMode: All` does not specify a count\n- Called for both `ExactDeviceRequest` (line 261) and `DeviceSubRequest` (line 250)\n\n### Quota Evaluator\n\n**File: `pkg/quota/v1/evaluator/core/resource_claims.go:249-277`**\n- For `DeviceAllocationModeAll`, assumes worst-case `AllocationResultsMaxSize` devices for quota purposes (lines 250-251, 275-277)\n- This is unchanged by the commit, but becomes more impactful if multi-node pools expose more devices per claim\n\n### Kubelet DRA Manager\n\n**File: `pkg/kubelet/cm/dra/manager.go:237-320`**\n- `prepareResources()` processes the allocation result received from the scheduler\n- It calls `NodePrepareResources` on the DRA plugin for each claim\n- The kubelet is allocation-mode agnostic \u2014 it only processes the final `AllocationResult`\n\n### Node Selector Construction\n\n**File: `staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/stable/allocator_stable.go:1377-1420`**\n- `createNodeSelector()` at line 1379 constructs the node affinity for the allocation\n- When `NodeName` is set on a device/slice (line 1397), the allocation is pinned to that specific node\n- This is the mechanism that constrains `AllocationMode: All` results to node-local devices\n\n### Test Coverage\n\n**File: `staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/allocatortesting/allocator_testing.go`**\n- `\"allocation-mode-all-with-multi-host-resource-pool\"` test at line 5093 (added by the commit): tests that a pool spanning two nodes (node1, node2) with `AllocationMode: All` only allocates device1 from node1 (not device2 from node2)\n- `\"all-devices-single\"` at line 1218: single device with All mode\n- `\"all-devices-many\"` at line 1235: multiple pools, All mode\n- `\"all-devices-of-the-incomplete-pool\"` at line 1256: verifies incomplete pools are rejected for All mode\n- `\"all-devices-plus-another\"` at line 1279: All mode combined with ExactCount\n\n**Other test files referencing AllocationMode:**\n- `pkg/apis/resource/validation/validation_resourceclaim_test.go:462-481` \u2014 validation tests\n- `pkg/registry/resource/resourceclaim/strategy_test.go:50-106`\n- `pkg/registry/resource/resourceclaimtemplate/strategy_test.go:49-96`\n- `pkg/quota/v1/evaluator/core/resource_claims_test.go:511-593`\n- `pkg/api/resourceclaimspec/util_test.go:45-47`\n- `pkg/registry/resource/resourceclaim/declarative_validation_test.go:516-550`\n- `pkg/apis/resource/fuzzer/fuzzer.go:39-52`\n\n### Performance Test Configuration\n\n**File: `test/integration/scheduler_perf/dra/performance-config.yaml`**\n- `SchedulingWithResourceClaimTemplate` benchmarks with 5000 nodes \u00d7 10 claims/node = 50,000 slices\n- The change adds O(50,000) additional work per `Filter` call in the `GatherPools` pre-scan\n- For 500 nodes with 2500 measure pods, this means ~500 \u00d7 2500 = 1.25M additional slice iterations\n\n### Commit History\n\n- **2e534d6** (2025-10-08, Morten Torkildsen): Original change \"DRA: Allow AllocationMode: All from multi-node resource pools\"\n- **83504f1** (2025-10-31): Merge of PR #134466\n- **a0e500a** (2025-11-03, Patrick Ohly): Revert \u2014 \"This reverts commit 2e534d6da100. It caused a performance regression, a different fix is needed.\"\n\n## Affected Components\n\n### HIGH RISK \u2014 Performance-Critical (Scheduler Hot Path)\n\n| Package | File | Impact |\n|---------|------|--------|\n| `structured/internal/stable` | `pools_stable.go:48-148` | GatherPools pre-scan of all slices runs per-node in Filter; O(S) per Filter call |\n| `structured/internal/incubating` | `pools_incubating.go` | Same GatherPools change |\n| `structured/internal/experimental` | `pools_experimental.go` | Same GatherPools change |\n| `structured/internal/stable` | `allocator_stable.go:110-134,446-481` | Allocate() entry point + AllocationMode handling |\n| `scheduler/framework/plugins/dynamicresources` | `dynamicresources.go:631-744` | Filter() calls Allocate() per-node |\n\n### MEDIUM RISK \u2014 Correctness-Sensitive (Allocation Logic)\n\n| Package | File | Impact |\n|---------|------|--------|\n| `structured/internal/stable` | `allocator_stable.go:856-914` | \"doAllDevices\" allocation loop \u2014 if pool boundary changes, wrong device set may be allocated |\n| `structured/internal/stable` | `allocator_stable.go:1377-1420` | createNodeSelector \u2014 multi-node pools may produce different node constraints |\n| `quota/v1/evaluator/core` | `resource_claims.go:249-277` | Quota evaluation assumes max devices for All mode; more devices per claim if pools span nodes |\n| `apis/resource/validation` | `validation.go:267-286` | No change needed, but validates AllocationMode is well-formed |\n\n### LOW RISK \u2014 Downstream Consumers (Allocation-Mode Agnostic)\n\n| Package | File | Impact |\n|---------|------|--------|\n| `kubelet/cm/dra` | `manager.go:237-320` | Processes allocation result; agnostic to AllocationMode \u2014 sees only final device list |\n| `kubelet/cm` | `container_manager_linux.go:134` | Holds reference to DRA manager |\n| `client-go/applyconfigurations/resource/v1` | `exactdevicerequest.go`, `devicesubrequest.go` | Generated apply config builders \u2014 no logic change |\n| `client-go/applyconfigurations/resource/v1beta1` | Multiple files | Same \u2014 generated code |\n| `client-go/applyconfigurations/resource/v1beta2` | Multiple files | Same \u2014 generated code |\n| `api/resource/v1` | `types.go`, `generated.proto` | Type definitions only |\n\n### NOT AFFECTED \u2014 No Behavioral Change\n\n| Package | File | Reason |\n|---------|------|--------|\n| `apis/resource/fuzzer` | `fuzzer.go` | Fuzz testing helper |\n| `api/resourceclaimspec` | `util_test.go` | Test data only |\n| E2E test driver | `test/e2e/dra/test-driver/app/kubeletplugin.go` | Test infrastructure |\n\n## Recommendation\n\n### Risk Assessment\n\nThe change was **already reverted** (a0e500a) due to a confirmed performance regression. The fundamental issue is an architectural mismatch: the correctness requirement (global pool completeness for `AllocationMode: All`) conflicts with the performance requirement (per-node Filter must be fast).\n\n**What could break if this change has bugs:**\n1. **Performance regression (confirmed):** The O(S) pre-scan in `GatherPools` runs per-node during Filter, scaling with total cluster slice count. In a 5000-node cluster with 10 slices/node, this adds 50,000 iterations per Filter call.\n2. **False incomplete pool detection:** If the `incompletePools` set incorrectly marks a pool as incomplete (e.g., due to stale generation data), `AllocationMode: All` claims would fail allocation even when devices are available on the target node.\n3. **Over-allocation from multi-node pools:** If `DeviceSlicesTargetingNode` is not correctly filtered for the target node, `AllocationMode: All` could attempt to allocate devices not available on the scheduled node, leading to kubelet NodePrepareResources failures.\n4. **Quota over-counting:** Multi-node pools exposing more devices per-node could cause quota evaluator to over-count, though the worst-case `AllocationResultsMaxSize` assumption already handles this conservatively.\n\n### Recommended Testing Plan\n\n1. **Performance benchmarks (mandatory before re-landing):**\n   - Run `SchedulingWithResourceClaimTemplate/5000pods_500nodes` from `test/integration/scheduler_perf/dra/performance-config.yaml`\n   - Compare scheduling throughput before/after the change\n   - Target: no more than 10% regression vs baseline (current threshold: 40 pods/sec)\n\n2. **Unit tests (already present, extend for edge cases):**\n   - The `\"allocation-mode-all-with-multi-host-resource-pool\"` test in `allocator_testing.go` covers the basic case\n   - Add tests for: incomplete multi-node pools, multi-node pools with mixed generations, multi-node pools with `PerDeviceNodeSelection`\n\n3. **Integration tests:**\n   - Test scheduling with `AllocationMode: All` claims where pools span 2+ nodes\n   - Verify that only node-local devices are allocated\n   - Verify that incomplete multi-node pools correctly block allocation\n\n4. **E2E tests:**\n   - The `multiNodeTests` function in `test/e2e/dra/dra.go:1150` provides the multi-node test framework\n   - Add a test case that creates a multi-node resource pool and verifies `AllocationMode: All` allocates correctly\n\n### Risk Mitigation Strategy\n\nThe correct fix should avoid the per-node O(S) pre-scan. # Investigation Report

## Summary

The change to allow `AllocationMode: All` from multi-node resource pools (commit 2e534d6) modifies the `GatherPools` function in the DRA structured allocator to pre-compute pool completeness across **all** slices (including those not targeting the current node) before filtering. This affects the scheduler's Filter extension point hot path, where `Allocate()` is called for every candidate node. The change was already reverted (commit a0e500a) due to a confirmed performance regression, indicating that the current approach of iterating all slices upfront in `GatherPools` is too expensive for the scheduler's per-node evaluation loop.

## Root Cause

The change modifies `GatherPools` in three allocator variants (stable, incubating, experimental) to:

1. **Pre-index all slices by pool** (`slicesByPool` map) before any node filtering, adding an O(S) pass over all slices where S = total slices in the cluster.
2. **Pre-compute incomplete pools** by checking slice counts and generations across all slices per pool, adding another O(S) pass.
3. **Change the `IsIncomplete` check** from a local per-pool check (`len(pool.Slices) != ResourceSliceCount`) to a lookup into the pre-computed `incompletePools` set.

The core problem: previously, `GatherPools` would only process slices matching the target node. The change forces it to process **all** slices to determine global pool completeness, which is necessary for correctness (a multi-node pool with `AllocationMode: All` needs to know if the pool is complete globally, not just for one node's slices). However, this work scales with the total number of ResourceSlices in the cluster, not just those relevant to a node, and it runs on **every** `Filter` call — i.e., for every (pod, node) pair during scheduli
... (truncated)
